if (!is_file('res/OIDplus/acknowledgements$dede.html')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: res/OIDplus/acknowledgements$dede.html');
	writefile_2();
	if (!is_file('res/OIDplus/acknowledgements$dede.html')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): res/OIDplus/acknowledgements$dede.html');
	} else if (sha1_file('res/OIDplus/acknowledgements$dede.html') != '23156db9ab96037bf24a87b1ff08fbb0d8fc8a70') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): res/OIDplus/acknowledgements$dede.html');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('res/OIDplus/acknowledgements$dede.html', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of res/OIDplus/acknowledgements$dede.html');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('res/OIDplus/acknowledgements$dede.html') !== '23156db9ab96037bf24a87b1ff08fbb0d8fc8a70') {
		if (@sha1_file('res/OIDplus/acknowledgements$dede.html') !== '96589ec09fa7215e575e09e3d5a9e0a1e419c59a') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: res/OIDplus/acknowledgements$dede.html');
			$tmp = pathinfo('res/OIDplus/acknowledgements$dede.html');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('res/OIDplus/acknowledgements$dede.html')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('res/OIDplus/acknowledgements$dede.html', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_2();
		if (@sha1_file('res/OIDplus/acknowledgements$dede.html') !== '23156db9ab96037bf24a87b1ff08fbb0d8fc8a70') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): res/OIDplus/acknowledgements$dede.html');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('res/OIDplus/acknowledgements.html')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: res/OIDplus/acknowledgements.html');
	writefile_3();
	if (!is_file('res/OIDplus/acknowledgements.html')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): res/OIDplus/acknowledgements.html');
	} else if (sha1_file('res/OIDplus/acknowledgements.html') != '252009260ea841fd50c107be0d10a8e6973ddd92') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): res/OIDplus/acknowledgements.html');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('res/OIDplus/acknowledgements.html', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of res/OIDplus/acknowledgements.html');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('res/OIDplus/acknowledgements.html') !== '252009260ea841fd50c107be0d10a8e6973ddd92') {
		if (@sha1_file('res/OIDplus/acknowledgements.html') !== '2dffbc691beb081b28f91245b809f98e74984f5c') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: res/OIDplus/acknowledgements.html');
			$tmp = pathinfo('res/OIDplus/acknowledgements.html');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('res/OIDplus/acknowledgements.html')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('res/OIDplus/acknowledgements.html', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_3();
		if (@sha1_file('res/OIDplus/acknowledgements.html') !== '252009260ea841fd50c107be0d10a8e6973ddd92') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): res/OIDplus/acknowledgements.html');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('res/OIDplus/privacy_documentation$dede.html')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: res/OIDplus/privacy_documentation$dede.html');
	writefile_4();
	if (!is_file('res/OIDplus/privacy_documentation$dede.html')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): res/OIDplus/privacy_documentation$dede.html');
	} else if (sha1_file('res/OIDplus/privacy_documentation$dede.html') != '7990187a3f7d6cdd61183841a10fbcb746dfec5a') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): res/OIDplus/privacy_documentation$dede.html');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('res/OIDplus/privacy_documentation$dede.html', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of res/OIDplus/privacy_documentation$dede.html');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('res/OIDplus/privacy_documentation$dede.html') !== '7990187a3f7d6cdd61183841a10fbcb746dfec5a') {
		if (@sha1_file('res/OIDplus/privacy_documentation$dede.html') !== '1beddaab4cfff31ad4fea516c394366e4c63afc6') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: res/OIDplus/privacy_documentation$dede.html');
			$tmp = pathinfo('res/OIDplus/privacy_documentation$dede.html');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('res/OIDplus/privacy_documentation$dede.html')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('res/OIDplus/privacy_documentation$dede.html', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_4();
		if (@sha1_file('res/OIDplus/privacy_documentation$dede.html') !== '7990187a3f7d6cdd61183841a10fbcb746dfec5a') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): res/OIDplus/privacy_documentation$dede.html');
		}
	}
}

	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: res/OIDplus/privacy_documentation.html');
	writefile_5();
	if (!is_file('res/OIDplus/privacy_documentation.html')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): res/OIDplus/privacy_documentation.html');
	} else if (sha1_file('res/OIDplus/privacy_documentation.html') != 'f20c75f719807c445431a946d38078ccd2f0c92e') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): res/OIDplus/privacy_documentation.html');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('res/OIDplus/privacy_documentation.html', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of res/OIDplus/privacy_documentation.html');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('res/OIDplus/privacy_documentation.html') !== 'f20c75f719807c445431a946d38078ccd2f0c92e') {
		if (@sha1_file('res/OIDplus/privacy_documentation.html') !== '4b0fa81e71f9895e91fe04e41961d2bcf3e3cfaf') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: res/OIDplus/privacy_documentation.html');
			$tmp = pathinfo('res/OIDplus/privacy_documentation.html');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('res/OIDplus/privacy_documentation.html')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('res/OIDplus/privacy_documentation.html', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_5();
		if (@sha1_file('res/OIDplus/privacy_documentation.html') !== 'f20c75f719807c445431a946d38078ccd2f0c92e') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): res/OIDplus/privacy_documentation.html');
		}
	}
}
